        <script type="text/javascript">
         var ajaxSuggestUrl = "https:\/\/www.tintworld.com\/store\/catalogsearch\/ajax\/suggest";
jQuery(function ($) {
    $('#js-wp-header-store-search-input').on('input', function (event) {
        var self = this;

        if (self.value.length > 2) {
            getAutocompleteValues(self.value);
        }
    });

    var getAutocompleteValues = function (input) {
        var promise = $.ajax({
            url : ajaxSuggestUrl,
            type: 'GET',
            data: {
                q: input
            }
        });

        promise.success(function (data) {
            var autocompleteSection = $('#js-wp-header-store-search-autocomplete')[0];
            if (data) {
                try {
                    autocompleteSection.innerHTML = data;
                } catch (e) {
                    // Do nothing
                }
            }
        });
    };
});
        </script>

           <button class="mini-dropdown-backdrop js-mini-dropdown-cart-backdrop js-mini-dropdown-close" type="button">
           </button>
           <div class="js-mini-dropdown-action mini-dropdown-action user-details" id="myCart">
            <ul class="list-unstyled">
             <span class="count">
              <span class="cartgo">
               0
              </span>
             </span>
             <li class="title">
              <span>
               My Cart
              </span>
             </li>
             <li class="data underline">
              <span>
               View Cart
              </span>
             </li>
             <li class="data yellow">
              Total :
              <span class="price">
               $0.00
              </span>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <div class="minicart-tooltip js-minicart-tooltip">
             <span class="minicart-empty-tooltip">
              Your cart is empty
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <script>
            jQuery(function ($) {
    var menuClass    = '.js-mini-dropdown-menu',
        tooltipClass = '.js-minicart-tooltip',
        overlayClass = '.js-mini-dropdown-cart-backdrop',
        overlay      = $(overlayClass),
        menu         = $(menuClass);

    overlay.detach().prependTo('.sitewrapper');

    function overlayClickHandler() {
        if (menu.hasClass('active')) {
            menu.removeClass('active');
            overlay.removeClass('active');
        }
    }

    setTimeout(function () {
        overlay.on('click', overlayClickHandler());
    }, 0);

    $('#myCart').on('click', function (event) {
        var self  = $(this),
            menu  = self.find(menuClass),
            count = 0;

        if (count === 0) {
            event.preventDefault();
            var tooltip = self.find(tooltipClass);
            menu.removeClass('active');
            overlay.removeClass('active');
            tooltip.addClass('active');
            setTimeout(function () {
                tooltip.removeClass('active');
            }, 2500);
        }
    });
});
           </script>

           <div class="js-mini-dropdown-action mini-dropdown-action user-details mini-garage-toggle" id="toggle3d79a39f57f5d71ac2df7f25dfc7a19b">
            <span class="mini-garage-count-wrapper">
             <span class="mini-garage-count">
              0
             </span>

             </li>
             <li class="vehicle underline">
              No Vehicle Selected
             </li>
            </ul>
            <div class="js-mini-dropdown-menu mini-dropdown-menu my-garage">
             <button class="mini-dropdown-backdrop js-mini-dropdown-close" type="button">
             </button>
             <div class="mini-dropdown-header">
              <span class="header-icon">
               <span class="mini-garage-count">
                0
               </span>
               <img class="garage" src="https://www.tintworld.com/store/skin/frontend/boilerplate/tintworld/images/mini-garage-icon.png"/>
              </span>
              <div class="header-title-content">
               <span class="header-title">
                My Garage
               </span>
              </div>
              <span class="js-mini-dropdown-close header-close-icon fa fa-chevron-up">
              </span>
             </div>
             <div class="mini-dropdown-main">
              <div class="mini-garage-message">
               <span class="mini-garage-empty-message">
                Garage is empty.
                <a class="js-scroll-to-shop-by-vehicle js-mini-dropdown-close" href="#">
                 Select a Vehicle
                </a>
                to store in your garage.
               </span>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
            <script>
             jQuery(function ($) {
    var container = $('#' + "garage3c289fae878e2ab182fe75848b2b3790"),
        form      = $('#' + null),
        toggle    = $('.js-mini-garage-toggle-wrapper');

    container.on('click', '.js-garage-vehicle-select', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var $this   = $(this),
            vehicle = $this.data('vehicle');

        if (vehicle.message) {
            alert(vehicle.message);
        } else {
                        form.find('[name=make]').val(vehicle.make).trigger('change', vehicle);
                    }

        return false;
    });

    container.on('click', '.js-garage-vehicle-delete', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var $this = $(this);

        jQuery.getJSON(
            $this.attr('href'),
            {},
            function (data) {
                if (true === data) {
                    $this.closest('.mini-garage-item').remove();
                } else {
                    alert(data);
                }
            }
        );

        return false;
    });

    $('.js-scroll-to-shop-by-vehicle').on('click', function(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var shopByYmm = $('#js-shop-by-vehicle');

        if (shopByYmm.length > 0) {
            $('html, body').animate({
                scrollTop: shopByYmm.offset().top - $('#mainheader').height
            }, 200);

            $('.mobile-nav-btn.active').removeClass('active');
            $('.mobile-nav-dropdown.active').removeClass('active');
            $(body).removeClass('noscroll');
        } else {
            $(location).attr('href', 'https://www.tintworld.com/store/?___SID=U ');
        }
    });

});
            </script>
           </div>

           <script>
            jQuery('#location-dropdown-form').on('submit', function (e) {
    e.preventDefault();

    jQuery.ajax({
        data   : jQuery(this).serialize(),
        type   : jQuery(this).attr('method'),
        url    : jQuery(this).attr('action'),
        success: function (data) {
            if (data) {
                var popup = jQuery('#location-popup');
                popup.show();
                jQuery('div.popup-inner.findstore').addClass('active');
                jQuery('#location-popup-search-list').html(data);
            } else {
                alert('Could not locate your address. Please enter more data and try again.');
            }
        },
        error  : function (request, status, error) {
            alert('Could not locate your address. Please enter more data and try again.');
        }
    });

    return false;
});

var autocomplete,
    options = {
        types                : ['(cities)'],
        componentRestrictions: {country: ['us', 'ca']}
    };

jQuery(function () {
    try {
        autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(document.getElementById('location-dropdown-autocomplete'), options);
    } catch (e) {
        // Do nothing
    }
});
           </script>

     <script>
      jQuery(function ($) {
    $('.js-scroll-to-shop-by-vehicle').on('click', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var shopByYmm = $('#js-shop-by-vehicle');

        if (shopByYmm.length > 0) {
            $('html, body').animate({
                scrollTop: shopByYmm.offset().top - $('#mainheader').height
            }, 200);

            $('.mobile-nav-btn.active').removeClass('active');
            $('.mobile-nav-dropdown.active').removeClass('active');
            $(body).removeClass('noscroll');
        } else {
            $(location).attr('href', 'https://www.tintworld.com/store/?___SID=U ');
        }
    });
});
     </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(function ($) {
    jQuery(function ($) {
        var brandsToggle    = $('.brands-toggle .brands-more'),
            brandsSecondary = $('.brands-container-secondary');

        brandsToggle.on('click', function (e) {
            if (!$(brandsSecondary).is(':visible')) {
                e.preventDefault();
                $(brandsSecondary).show();
                brandsToggle.html('View<br>All');
                brandsToggle.attr('href', '/store/brands/');
            }
        });
    });

    $.ajax({
        url: '/store/wordpress/index/category'
    }).success(function (data) {
        var categoryBlock = $(data).find('#homepage-main-category-slider');
        $('#homepage-category-slider').html(categoryBlock.html());
        $('#homepage-category-slider .regular').slick({
            dots          : true,
            infinite      : true,
            slidesToShow  : 4,
            slidesToScroll: 4,
            responsive    : [
                {
                    breakpoint: 1250,
                    settings  : {
                        slidesToShow  : 3,
                        slidesToScroll: 3,
                        infinite      : true,
                        dots          : true
                    }
                },
                {
                    breakpoint: 600,
                    settings  : {
                        slidesToShow  : 2,
                        slidesToScroll: 2
                    }
                },
                {
                    breakpoint: 480,
                    settings  : {
                        slidesToShow  : 1,
                        slidesToScroll: 1
                    }
                }
            ]
        });
    });
});

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function revslider_showDoubleJqueryError(sliderID) {
				var errorMessage = "Revolution Slider Error: You have some jquery.js library include that comes after the revolution files js include.";
				errorMessage += "<br> This includes make eliminates the revolution slider libraries, and make it not work.";
				errorMessage += "<br><br> To fix it you can:<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 1. In the Slider Settings -> Troubleshooting set option:  <strong><b>Put JS Includes To Body</b></strong> option to true.";
				errorMessage += "<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 2. Find the double jquery.js include and remove it.";
				errorMessage = "<span style='font-size:16px;color:#BC0C06;'>" + errorMessage + "</span>";
					jQuery(sliderID).show().html(errorMessage);
			}
   </script>

    var initLocationMap = function () {
        var locationSearchAction = "https:\/\/www.tintworld.com\/store\/location\/index\/popup\/?___SID=U",
            locationData         = {
                'address'         : "90 N Broadway,",
                'city'            : "Salem",
                'region'          : "New Hampshire",
                'country'         : "United States",
                'appointment_form': 1
            };

        jQuery('#location-popup-form').on('submit', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();

            jQuery.post(
                this.action,
                jQuery(this).serialize(),
                function (data) {
                    if (typeof data === typeof '') {
                        jQuery('#location-popup-search-list').html(data);
                    } else {
                        alert("Could not locate your address. Please enter more data and try again.");
                    }
                }
            );

            return false;
        });
    };
    initLocationMap();
   </script>
  </div>
  <script>
   jQuery(function ($) {
    var popup = $('#location-popup');

    popup.on('popup', function () {
        popup.show();
        $('div.popup-inner.findstore').addClass('active');
    });

    popup.on('click', '.close-popup', function () {
        popup.hide();
        $('div.popup-inner').removeClass('active');
        $('div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.popup-inner .messages').html('');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-time').hide();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-services').hide();
    });

    popup.on('click', 'div.popup-content a.closebtn', function () {
        popup.hide();
        $('div.popup-inner').removeClass('active');
        $('div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.popup-inner .messages').html('');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-time').hide();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-services').hide();
    });

    // Trigger for Quote Request Button
    popup.on('click', 'a.quoteRequest', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var dataID = $(this).data('id');
        var data   = {storeID: dataID};
        $.ajax({
            dataType: 'json',
            url     : 'https://www.tintworld.com/wp-content/themes/tintworld_dev/assign-store-scheduler.php',
            type    : 'POST',
            data    : data,
            success : function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
                $('div.storeinfo').load('https://www.tintworld.com/wp-content/themes/tintworld_dev/storeinfo.php');
                $('div.popup-inner').removeClass('active');
                $('div.popup-inner.quoteRequest').addClass('active');
                $('div.popup-inner.quoteRequest div.stepone').addClass('active');
            },
            error   : function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(errorThrown);
            }
        });
    });

    // Trigger for title link in My Store
    $('div#myStore').on('click', 'li.title', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.popup-inner.findstore').addClass('active');
    });

    // Trigger for Appointment Request Button
    popup.on('click', 'a.appointmentRequest', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var dataID = $(this).data('id');
        var data   = {storeID: dataID};
        $.ajax({
            dataType: 'json',
            url     : 'https://www.tintworld.com/wp-content/themes/tintworld_dev/assign-store-scheduler.php',
            type    : 'POST',
            data    : data,
            success : function (data, textStatus, jqXHR) {
                $('div.storeinfo').load('https://www.tintworld.com/wp-content/themes/tintworld_dev/storeinfo.php');
                $('div.popup-inner').removeClass('active');
                $('div.popup-inner.appointmentRequest').addClass('active');
                $('div.popup-inner.appointmentRequest div.stepone').addClass('active');
            },
            error   : function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                console.log(errorThrown);
            }
        });
    });

    // Next button on "step one" window of Appointment Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.stepone a.next', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Validation
        if ($('div.appointmentRequest div.stepone input[type=radio]:checked').length > 0) {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo').addClass('active');

            // Set value of hidden input field for service type
            var serviceType = $('div.appointmentRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val();
            $('form#appointment-request input[name="service-department"]').val(serviceType);

            if ($('div.appointmentRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Automotive') {
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.automotive').addClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour div.vehicleFields').show();
            } else if ($('div.appointmentRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Residential') {
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.residential').addClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour div.vehicleFields').hide();
            } else if ($('div.appointmentRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Commercial') {
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.commercial').addClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour div.vehicleFields').hide();
            } else if ($('div.appointmentRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Marine') {
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.marine').addClass('active');
                $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour div.vehicleFields').hide();
            }

            // Reset services checkboxes, so that we only show their current services
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo input[type=checkbox]:checked').prop('checked', false);

        } else {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepone div.messages').html('<div class=\'alert alert-danger\'>Please select a service type to proceed.</div>');
        }
    });

    // Next button on "step one" window of Quote Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.quoteRequest div.stepone a.next', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Validation
        if ($('div.quoteRequest div.stepone input[type=radio]:checked').length > 0) {
            $('div.quoteRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
            $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo').addClass('active');

            // Set value of hidden input field for service type
            var serviceType = $('div.quoteRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val();
            $('form#quote-request input[name="service-department"]').val(serviceType);

            if ($('div.quoteRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Automotive') {
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.automotive').addClass('active');
                $('div.quoteRequest div.stepthree div.vehicleFields').show();
            } else if ($('div.quoteRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Residential') {
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.residential').addClass('active');
            } else if ($('div.quoteRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Commercial') {
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.commercial').addClass('active');
            } else if ($('div.quoteRequest input[name="service"]:checked').val() == 'Marine') {
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.services').removeClass('active');
                $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.marine').addClass('active');
            }

            // Reset services checkboxes, so that we only show their current services
            $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo input[type=checkbox]:checked').prop('checked', false);

        } else {
            $('div.quoteRequest div.stepone div.messages').html('<div class=\'alert alert-danger\'>Please select a service type to proceed.</div>');
        }
    });

    // Next button on "step two" window of Appointment Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo a.next', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Validation
        if ($('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo input[type=checkbox]:checked').length > 0) {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree').addClass('active');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.messages').html('');
            $('div.appointmentRequest .appointment-days').slick('resize');

            // Store selected services in a variable, and write it to the DIV
            var names = $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo input[type=checkbox]:checked').map(function () {
                return this.value;
            }).get().join(', ');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-services p.services').html(names);
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.popup-content div.selected-services').show();
            $('form#appointment-request input[name="services_appt"]').val(names);
        } else {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo div.messages').html('<div class=\'alert alert-danger\'>Please select at least one service to proceed.</div>');
        }
    });

    // Next button on "step two" window of Quote Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.quoteRequest div.steptwo a.next', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Validation
        if ($('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo input[type=checkbox]:checked').length > 0) {
            $('div.quoteRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
            $('div.quoteRequest div.stepthree').addClass('active');
            $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.messages').html('');

            // Store selected services in a variable, and write it to the DIV
            var names = $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo input[type=checkbox]:checked').map(function () {
                return this.value;
            }).get().join(', ');
            $('div.quoteRequest div.selected-services p.services').html(names);
            $('div.quoteRequest div.popup-content div.selected-services').show();
            $('form#quote-request input[name="services"]').val(names);
        } else {
            $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo div.messages').html('<div class=\'alert alert-danger\'>Please select at least one service to proceed.</div>');
        }
    });

    // Next button on "step three" window of Appointment Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree a.next', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        // Validation
        if (($('div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree div.appointment-days').find('a.active').length !== 0) && ($('div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree div.availableAppointments').find('a.active').length !== 0)) {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour').addClass('active');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree div.messages').html('');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.popup-content div.selected-time').show();
        } else {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree div.messages').html('<div class=\'alert alert-danger\'>Please select a date and time to proceed.</div>');
        }
    });

    // Submit Button on Quote Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.quoteRequest div.stepthree a.next', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Validation
        var empty = true;
        $('div.quoteRequest div.stepthree input[type="text"]').each(function () {
            if ($(this).val() != '') {
                empty = false;
                return false;
            } else {
                empty = true;
            }
        });

        if (empty == true) {
            $('div.quoteRequest div.stepthree div.messages').html('<div class=\'alert alert-danger\'>Please complete all of the fields below.</div>');
        } else {
            $('div.quoteRequest div.stepthree div.messages').html('');
            $('div.quoteRequest div.stepthree a.next').html('Submitting <i class="fa fa-spinner fa-spin fa-1x fa-fw"></i>');
            $.ajax({
                type    : 'POST',
                url     : 'https://www.tintworld.com/wp-content/themes/tintworld_dev/assets/forms/process.php',
                dataType: 'json',
                data    : $('div.quoteRequest form#quote-request').serialize(),
                success : function (result) {
                    $('div.quoteRequest div.stepthree a.next').html('Get Quote <i class="fa fa-chevron-right" aria-hidden="true"></i>');
                    $('div.quoteRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
                    $('div.quoteRequest div.stepfour').addClass('active');
                }
            });
        }
    });

    // Submit Button on Appointment Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour a.next', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        // Validation
        var empty = true;
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour input[type="text"]').each(function () {
            if ($(this).val() != '') {
                empty = false;
                return false;
            } else {
                empty = true;
            }
        });

        if (empty == true) {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour div.messages').html('<div class=\'alert alert-danger\'>Please complete all of the fields below.</div>');
        } else {
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour div.messages').html('');
            $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour a.next').html('Submitting <i class="fa fa-spinner fa-spin fa-1x fa-fw"></i>');
            $.ajax({
                type    : 'POST',
                url     : 'https://www.tintworld.com/wp-content/themes/tintworld_dev/assets/forms/process.php',
                dataType: 'json',
                data    : $('div.appointmentRequest form#appointment-request').serialize(),
                success : function (result) {
                    $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour a.next').html('Get Appointment <i class="fa fa-chevron-right" aria-hidden="true"></i>');
                    $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
                    $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepfive').addClass('active');
                }
            });
        }
    });

    // Back button on "step four" window of Appointment Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.stepfour a.back', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree').addClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.popup-content div.selected-time').hide();
    });

    // Back button on "step three" window of Appointment Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree a.back', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo').addClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.popup-content div.selected-services').hide();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-services p.services').html('');
    });

    // Back button on "step two" window of Appointment Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo a.back', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepone').addClass('active');
    });

    // Back button on "step three" window of Quote Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.quoteRequest div.stepthree a.back', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.quoteRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo').addClass('active');
        $('div.quoteRequest div.popup-content div.selected-services').hide();
        $('div.quoteRequest div.selected-services p.services').html('');
    });

    // Back button on "step two" window of Quote Request
    popup.on('click', 'div.quoteRequest div.steptwo a.back', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.quoteRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.quoteRequest div.stepone').addClass('active');
    });

    // Back Button on "step one" window
    popup.on('click', 'div.stepone a.back', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.popup-inner').removeClass('active');
        $('div.popup-inner.findstore').addClass('active');
    });

    // Services Edit Button on Appointment Windows
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.selected-services h4 a', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.steptwo').addClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-services p.services').html('');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-services').hide();
    });

    // Services Edit Button on Quote Windows
    popup.on('click', 'div.quoteRequest div.selected-services h4 a', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.quoteRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.quoteRequest div.steptwo').addClass('active');
        $('div.quoteRequest div.selected-services p.services').html('');
        $('div.quoteRequest div.selected-services').hide();
    });

    // Appointment Edit Button on Appointment Windows
    popup.on('click', 'div.appointmentRequest div.selected-time h4 a', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.step').removeClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.stepthree').addClass('active');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-time').hide();
    });

    // Click event for appointment time (Date)
    popup.on('click', 'div.popup-content .slick-slide a', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.popup-content .slick-slide a').removeClass('active');
        $(this).addClass('active');

        // Load the availableappointments based on the selected store, and the day selected
        var day = $(this).data('day');
        $('div.availableAppointments').load('https://www.tintworld.com/wp-content/themes/tintworld_dev/fetch-appointments.php?day=' + day);

        var dateSelected = $(this).data('datefull');
        $('form#appointment-request input[name="appointmentDate"]').val(dateSelected);
    });

    // Click event for appointment time (Time)
    popup.on('click', 'div.popup-content ul.appointments li a', function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $('div.popup-content ul.appointments li a').removeClass('active');
        $(this).addClass('active');

        var timeSelected = '@' + $(this).data('time');
        $('div.appointmentRequest div.selected-time p.appointment-time').html(timeSelected);
        $('form#appointment-request input[name="appointmentTime"]').val($(this).data('time'));
    });

    $('section#topbar ul').on('click', 'li.popup a', function () {
        popup.show();
        $('div.popup-inner.findstore').addClass('active');
    });

    $('.appointment-days').slick({
        dots          : false,
        infinite      : false,
        slidesToShow  : 7,
        slidesToScroll: 7,
        responsive    : [
            {
                breakpoint: 1024,
                settings  : {
                    slidesToShow  : 3,
                    slidesToScroll: 3,
                    infinite      : true,
                    dots          : false
                }
            },
            {
                breakpoint: 600,
                settings  : {
                    slidesToShow  : 2,
                    slidesToScroll: 2
                }
            },
            {
                breakpoint: 480,
                settings  : {
                    slidesToShow  : 1,
                    slidesToScroll: 1
                }
            }
        ]
    });
});

// This example requires the Places library. Include the libraries=places
// parameter when you first load the API. For example:
// <script src="https://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?key=YOUR_API_KEY&libraries=places">

var placeSearch, autocomplete;
var componentForm = {
    street_number              : 'short_name',

    locality                   : 'long_name',

    postal_code                : 'short_name'
};

    types                : ['(cities)'],
    componentRestrictions: {country: ['us', 'ca', 'sa']}
};

jQuery(function () {
    autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(document.getElementById('autocomplete'), options);
});
